<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">DIRECTORS&#146; REPORT</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Your Directors submit the financial report of Sundance
Energy Australia Limited (the &#147;Company&#148; or &#147;the consolidated 
group&#148;) for the half-year ended 30&nbsp;June&nbsp;2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-
weight:bold;">Directors</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The names of each person who has been a Director 
during the half-year and to the date of this report are:</font></p>

style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Michael D. Hannell &#151; Non-Executive 
Chairman</font></p>

CEO</font></p>

Director</font></p>

<td width="3%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF"

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Barrel of oil 
equivalent (Boe) and average net daily production (Boe/d).</font></b>&#160; 
Sales volume increased by 501,509 Boe (57.2%) to 1,377,984 Boe (7,613 Boe/d) for
the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 compared to 876,475 Boe (4,842 Boe/d) for
the same period in prior year due to successfully bringing online 52 gross (33.7
net) producing wells in the trailing twelve months (since 30 June&nbsp;2014), 
primarily in the Eagle Ford.&#160; Sales volume exclude 170,710 Boe (943 Boe/d) 
and 76,207 Boe (421 Boe/d) of flared production for the six-months ended 30 
June&nbsp;2015 and 2014, respectively.&#160; Including flared volumes, daily 
production was 8,556 Boe/d and 5,263 Boe/d for the six-months ended 30 
June&nbsp;2015 and 2014, respectively.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Eagle Ford contributed 6,296 Boe/d (82.7%) of 
total sales volume during the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 compared to 
2,642 Boe/d (54.6%) during the same period in prior year (a 138.3% year-over-
year increase). Mississippian/Woodford contributed 1,317 Boe/d (17.3%) of total 
sales volume during the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 compared to 1,366 
Boe/d (28.2%) during the same period in prior year. In the second-half of 2014, 
we disposed of our remaining interests in the Bakken Formation and DJ Basin 
assets, which collectively had 835 Boe/d (17.2%) of sales volume during the six-
months ended 30 June&nbsp;2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our sales volume is oil-weighted, with oil 
representing 74% and 73% of total sales volume for the six-months ended 30 
June&nbsp;2015 and 2014, respectively.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-
align:center;">1<a name="PB_1_213627_7056"></a></p>

align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='1',FILE='C:\JMS\brama\15-19269-1\task7584245\19269-1-mm-
01.htm',USER='105435',CD='Sep 11 21:51 2015' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Oil 
sales.</font></b>&#160; Oil sales decreased by $11.4 million (18.4%) to $50.3 
million for the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 from $61.7&nbsp;million for 
the same period in prior year. The decrease in oil revenues was the result of 
lower product pricing ($49.1 million), partially offset by increased oil 
production volumes ($37.7 million). Oil production volumes increased 61% to 
1,025,402 Bbls for the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 compared to 636,386 
Bbls for the same period in prior year. The average realised price on the sale 
of oil decreased by 49% to $49.10 per Bbl for the six-months ended 30 
June&nbsp;2015 from $96.99 per Bbl for the same period in prior year.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Natural gas 
sales.</font></b>&#160; Natural gas sales decreased by $1.1&nbsp;million (29.4%)
to $2.7&nbsp;million for the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 from $3.8 
million for the same period in prior year. The decrease in natural gas revenues 
was primarily the result of lower product pricing ($3.1 million), partially 
offset by increased production volumes ($2.0 million). Natural gas production 
volumes increased 412,576 Mcf (51.2%) to 1,217,927 Mcf for the six-months ended 
30 June&nbsp;2014 compared to 805,351 Mcf for the same period in prior year. The
average realised price on the sale of natural gas decreased by 53% to $2.22 per 
Mcf for the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 from $4.76 per Mcf for the same 
period in prior year.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NGL 
sales.</font></b>&#160; NGL sales decreased by $1.8&nbsp;million (46.7%) to $2.1
million for the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 from $3.9 million for the 
same period in prior year.&#160; The decrease in NGL revenues was primarily the 
result of lower product pricing ($3.4 million), partially offset by increased 
production volumes ($1.6 million).&#160; NGL production volumes increased 43,729
Bbls (41.3%) to 149,594 Bbls for the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 compared
to 105,865 Bbls for the same period in prior year. The average realised price on
the sale of natural gas liquids decreased by 62% to $13.75 per Bbl for the six-
months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 from $36.45 per Bbl for the same period in prior 
year.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>    </td>
<td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.5%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font 
size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-
weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>    </td>
<td width="26%" colspan="5" valign="bottom" style="border:none;border-
bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:26.5%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font

face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.56</font></p>    </td>
<td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.5%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="12%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:12.0%;">
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2"

<td width="3%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:3.0%;">

(costs)</font></p>    </td>
<td width="2%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF"

<td width="2%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF"

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">)</font></p>    </td>
<td width="12%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF"

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2"
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>    </td>
<td width="3%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF"

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Lease 
operating expenses.</font></b>&#160; Lease operating expenses (LOE) increased by
$2.3&nbsp;million (35.3%) to $8.8&nbsp;million for the six-months ended 30 
June&nbsp;2015 from $6.5&nbsp;million for the same period in prior year but 
decreased $1.03 per Boe to $6.36 per Boe from $7.39 per Boe. The decrease in LOE
per Boe is primarily due to the implementation of several changes in our field 
operation and a higher concentration of production in lower cost operating 
areas.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Production 
taxes.</font></b>&#160; Production taxes decreased by $0.8&nbsp;million (19.2%) 
to $3.2&nbsp;million for the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 due to lower 
overall revenue, but stayed relatively flat as a percent of revenue (5.9% 
compared to 5.8% in the prior period.)</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Depreciation 
and amortisation expense, including depletion.</font></b>&#160; Depreciation and
amortisation expense increased by $17.7&nbsp;million (56.7%) to 
$48.8&nbsp;million for the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 from 
$31.2&nbsp;million for the same period in prior year. The increase is in-line 
with our production increase (57.2%).</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">General and 
administrative expenses.</font></b>&#160; General and administrative expenses 
decreased by $0.5 million (5.2%) to $8.8 million for the six-months ended 30 
June&nbsp;2015 from $9.3 million for the same period in prior year.&#160; 
G&amp;A per Boe decreased by 39.7% to $6.38 for the six-months ended 30 
June&nbsp;2015 as compared to $10.58 per Boe for the same period in prior year. 
The decrease in general and administrative expenses per Boe is driven by lower 
overall costs combined with increased production levels.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-
align:center;">2<a name="PB_2_213640_5335"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade
align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\JMS\brama\15-19269-1\task7584245\19269-1-mm-
01.htm',USER='105435',CD='Sep 11 21:51 2015' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Impairment 
expense.</font></b>&#160; Impairment expense of $16.0 million for the six-months
ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 was related to the write-down of the Company&#146;s 
Mississippian/Woodford development and production assets ($2.6 million) and 
exploration and evaluation expenditures ($13.4 million).&#160; The impairment is
primarily the result of a prolonged decrease in commodity pricing, which has 
decreased the fair value of the Company&#146;s oil and gas assets.&#160; The 
Company did not record an impairment of its Eagle Ford assets as at 30 
June&nbsp;2015.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Finance 
costs.</font></b> Finance costs, net of amounts capitalised to exploration and 
development, increased by $1.6&nbsp;million to $2.4 million for the six-months 
ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 as compared to $0.8&nbsp;million in the same period in 
prior year. The increase primarily relates to higher average outstanding credit 
facility amounts in the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 as compared to the 
same period in prior year.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Loss on 
derivative financial instruments.</font></b> The loss on derivative financial 
instruments decreased by $1.8&nbsp;million to a $0.5&nbsp;million loss for the 
six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 as compared to $2.2 million in the same 
period in prior year.&#160; The loss on commodity hedging consisted of $5.6 
million of unrealised losses on commodity derivative contracts, offset by $5.1 
million of realised gains on commodity derivative contracts.&#160; The Company 
paid $0.7 million for commodity derivative contracts in the six-months ended 30 
June&nbsp;2015.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Adjusted 
EBITDAX</font></b>.&#160; Adjusted EBITDAX is defined as earnings before 
interest expense, debt extinguishment costs, income taxes, depreciation, 
depletion and amortisation, property impairments, gain/(loss) on sale of non-
current assets, exploration expense, share-based compensation and gains and 
losses on commodity hedging, net of settlements of commodity hedging.&#160; For 
the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015, adjusted EBITDAX was $41.3 million, or 
75% of revenue, compared to $50.1 million, or 72% of revenue, from the same 
period in prior year.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following table presents a reconciliation of the 
profit (loss) attributable to owners of Sundance to Adjusted EBITDAX:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-
weight:bold;">Development</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s development activities are 
primarily focused in the Eagle Ford. Costs incurred for drilling and completions
during the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 totalled $39.1 million, which met 
the Company&#146;s down-cycle objective to manage the business within operating 
cash flows of $42.0 million.&#160; This investment resulted in the addition of 5
gross (4.0 net) Sundance operated wells into production.&#160; An additional 25 
gross (15.7 net) wells were drilling, being prepared for fracture stimulation or
testing as at 30 June&nbsp;2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015, the 
Company invested $12.6 million of capital expenditures related to the 
installation of a hydrogen sulphide (H2S) treatment facility to reduce or 
eliminate flared natural gas production, facilities and other development 
projects that are expected to reduce lease operating expenses, with an average 
project pay-back period of six months.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-
align:center;">3<a name="PB_3_213649_5796"></a></p>

align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='3',FILE='C:\JMS\brama\15-19269-1\task7584245\19269-1-mm-
01.htm',USER='105435',CD='Sep 11 21:51 2015' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-
weight:bold;">Exploration</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015, the 
Company acquired over 13,000 net Eagle Ford acres for approximately $14.1 
million, bringing its total Eagle Ford acreage to over 33,000 net acres 
(exclusive of the 5,500 net acres acquired from New Standard Energy Ltd).&#160; 
Mississippian/Woodford formation acreage additions during the period were 
immaterial and the Company expects to allow a significant number of leases to 
expire in the second half of 2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Acquisition of Oil 
and Gas Assets</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subsequent to 30 June&nbsp;2015, the Company completed
the acquisition of New Standard Energy Ltd&#146;s (NSE) U.S (Eagle Ford assets) 
and Cooper Basin assets (PEL570).&#160; The Eagle Ford assets acquired include 
approximately 5,500 net acres in Atascosa County, 7 gross producing wells with 
approximately 175 net Boe/d of current production and two wells that have been 
drilled but not yet completed. &#160;The Cooper Basin asset acquired is a 17.5% 
working interest in the PEL570 concession.&#160; Consideration for the 
acquisition included $15.0 million to repay NSE&#146;s note with Credit Suisse, 
the issuance of 6 million new fully paid ordinary Company shares and the 
assumption of net working capital deficit of approximately $0.9 million.&#160; 
Approximately 1.5 million of the 6 million Company shares will be held in escrow
until resolution of due diligence.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Financial 
Position</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">As at 30 June&nbsp;2015, the Company was in a strong 
financial position with $98.5 million of liquidity and a low leverage profile of
1.3x debt to trailing twelve-month Adjusted EBITDAX.&#160; The Company had oil 
derivative contracts covering 1,362,000 Bbls through 2019 with an average floor 
of and ceiling of $57.82 and $79.98, respectively.&#160; Of that 1,362,000 Bbls,
316,000 Bbls relate to second half 2015 and have an average floor of 
$66.74.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Auditor&#146;s 
Declaration</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

style="font-size:10.0pt;">The auditor&#146;s independence declaration as 
required under section 307C of the Corporations Act 2001 is set out on 
page&nbsp;5 for the half-year ended 30 June&nbsp;2015.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"

style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

style="font-size:10.0pt;">In relation to our review of the financial report of 
Sundance Energy Australia Limited for the half-year ended 30 June&nbsp;2015, to 
the best of my knowledge and belief, there have been no contraventions of the 
auditor independence requirements of the <i>Corporations Act 2001</i> or any 
applicable code of professional conduct.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"

June&nbsp;2015</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NOTE 1 - BASIS OF 
PREPARATION</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The general purpose financial statements for the 
interim half-year reporting period ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 have been prepared in
accordance with the Corporations Act 2001 and Australian Accounting Standards 
Board (AASB) 134 Interim Financial Reporting.&#160; Compliance with AASB 134 
ensures that the financial statements and notes also comply with International 
Accounting Standards (IAS) 34 Interim Financial Reporting, as issued by the 
International Accounting Standards Board (IASB).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The interim consolidated financial statements do not 
include all the information and disclosures required in the annual financial 
statements, and should be read in conjunction with the Company&#146;s annual 
financial statements as at 31 December&nbsp;2014 and any public announcements
made by the Company during the interim reporting period in accordance with the 
continuous disclosure requirements of the Corporations Act 2001.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The accounting policies and methods of computation 
that are discussed in Note 1 of the Company&#146;s 31 December&nbsp;2014 annual 
financial statements have been consistently applied to the half-year reporting 
period ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 unless otherwise stated.&#160; The Company has 
adopted all new accounting standards and amendments issued by the AASB and the 
IASB that became mandatorily applicable as at 1 January&nbsp;2015.&#160; There 
was no material impact from the adoption of these standards.&#160; The Company 
did not adopt any of the standards that have been issued by the AASB and the 
IASB, but were not mandatorily applicable during the period and is in the 
process of accessing the impact of adopting such standards.&#160; Certain prior 
period comparatives have been reclassified to conform to the current 
period&#146;s presentation.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The consolidated financial statements and accompanying
notes are presented in U.S. dollars and all values are rounded to the nearest 
thousand (US$&#146;000), except where stated otherwise.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NOTE 5 &#151; INCOME TAX 
BENEFIT</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the six-months ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 the 
Company recognised an income tax benefit of $12.2 million on a pre-tax loss of 
$33.9 million, representing 36% of pre-tax loss.&#160; The difference between 
the prima facie tax benefit of $2.0 million at the Company&#146;s statutory 
income tax rate of 30% is primarily due to the impact of foreign tax 
rates.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NOTE 6 &#151; IMPAIRMENT OF NON-
CURRENT ASSETS</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">At 30 June&nbsp;2015, the Group reassessed the 
carrying amount of its non-current assets for indicators of impairment or 
whether there is any indication that an impairment loss may no longer exist or 
may have decreased in accordance with the Group&#146;s accounting 
policy.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">As at 30 June&nbsp;2015, the Company determined there 
was:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-
indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>an indication of impairment for its 
Mississippian/Woodford development and production assets due to the extended 
depressed oil pricing environment and the Company&#146;s expected use of those 
assets.</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-
indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>no indication that the impairment 
loss related to its Eagle Ford development and production assets no longer
existed as there was not significant change in the asset&#146;s value or how the
Company uses those assets.</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-
indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>an indication of impairment for its 
Mississippian/Woodford exploration and evaluation expenditures due to the fact 
that a significant amount of its leases will expire in the near future and are 
not expected to be renewed.</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-
indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>no indication of impairment for its 
Eagle Ford exploration and evaluation expenditures.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">As at 31 December&nbsp;2014, there was no indication 
that the Company&#146;s Mississippian/Woodford exploration and evaluation 
expenditures were impaired as the lower oil price environment had just begun and
there was not an expectation that leases set to expire in late 2015 would not be
renewed.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

align:center;">11<a name="PB_11_085531_2897"></a></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SUNDANCE ENERGY AUSTRALIA LIMITED ACN
112 202 883 AND CONTROLLED ENTITIES</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SELECTED EXPLANATORY NOTES TO THE 
FINANCIAL STATEMENTS</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">For the half-year ended 30 
June&nbsp;2015</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NOTE 6 &#151; IMPAIRMENT OF NON-
CURRENT ASSETS (CONT)</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each of the Group&#146;s development and production 
asset cash-generating units include all of its developed producing properties, 
shared infrastructure supporting its production and undeveloped acreage that the
Group considers technically feasible and commercially viable.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Estimates of recoverable amounts are based on the 
higher of an asset&#146;s value-in-use or fair value less costs to sell (level 3
fair value hierarchy), using a discounted cash flow method, and are most 
sensitive to the key assumptions such as pricing, discount rates, and reserve 
risk factors.&#160; For its development and production assets, the Group has 
used the FVLCS calculation whereby future cash flows are based on estimates of 
hydrocarbon reserves in addition to other relevant factors such as value 
attributable to additional reserves based on production plans.&#160; For its 
exploration and evaluation expenditures, the Group has used the FVLCS 
calculation determined by the probability weighted combination of a discounted 
cash flow method and market transactions for comparable undeveloped 
acreage.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Estimates of future commodity prices are based on the 
Group&#146;s best estimates of future market prices with reference to external 
market analysts&#146; forecasts, current spot prices and forward curves.&#160; 
At 30 June&nbsp;2015, future NYMEX strip prices, adjusted for basis 
differentials, were applied to the period from 1 July&nbsp;2015 to 30 
June&nbsp;2016 and gradually increased through the second half of 2016 and first
half of 2017 to $75/bbl as at 1 July&nbsp;2017 and thereafter.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The post-tax discount rate that has been applied to 
the development and production assets was 8.0%.&#160; The Group also applied 
further risk-adjustments appropriate for risks associated with its 
Mississippian/Woodford developed and undeveloped reserves using a risk-
adjustment rate of 5% and 30%, respectively, based on the risk associated with 
each reserve category.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The post-tax discount rate that has been applied to 
the exploration and evaluation expenditures was 15.0% and 20.0% for its probable
and possible reserves, respectively.&#160; The Group also applied further risk-
adjustments appropriate for risks associated with its Mississippian/Woodford 
probable and possible reserves using a risk-adjustment rate of 50% and 70%, 
respectively, based on the risk associated with each reserve 
category.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Recoverable amounts and resulting impairment write-
downs recognized in the statement of profit or loss and other comprehensive 
income for the six month period ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 are presented in the 
table below:</font></p>

style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">On May&nbsp;14, 2015, Sundance Energy Australia 
Limited and Sundance Energy,&nbsp;Inc. entered into a Credit Agreement (the 
&#147;Credit Agreement&#148;) with Morgan Stanley Energy Capital,&nbsp;Inc., as 
administrative agent (&#147;Agent&#148;) and the lenders from time to time party
thereto, which provides for a $300 million senior secured revolving credit 
facility (the &#147;Revolving Facility&#148;) and term loans of $125 million 
(the &#147;Term Loans), with an accordion feature providing for additional term 
loans of up to $50 million, subject to certain conditions.&#160; The Revolving 
Facility is subject to a borrowing base, which has been set initially at $75 
million. The Revolving Facility has a five year term (matures in May&nbsp;2020) 
and the Term Loans have a 5 &#189; year term (mature in 
November&nbsp;2020).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Revolving Facility and Term Loans refinanced the 
Company&#146;s credit facilities with Wells Fargo Bank, N.A. and Wells Fargo 
Energy Capital,&nbsp;Inc., respectively. At closing, the Company used $145.0 
million of the proceeds to pay off its previous credit facilities, which are 
fully paid-off. Approximately $1.1 million of deferred financing fees related to
the previous credit facilities were written off due to the refinance.&#160; In 
addition, the Company paid Wells Fargo et al $0.4 million of early termination 
fees at closing, for a total of $1.5 million of loss on debt extinguishment 
recorded in the statement of profit or loss and other comprehensive
income.</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SUNDANCE ENERGY AUSTRALIA LIMITED ACN
112 202 883 AND CONTROLLED ENTITIES</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SELECTED EXPLANATORY NOTES TO THE 
FINANCIAL STATEMENTS</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">For the half-year ended 30 
June&nbsp;2015</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NOTE 8 &#151; CREDIT FACILITIES 
(CONT)</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company is required under our Credit Agreement to 
maintain the following financial ratios:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-
indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>a minimum current ratio, consisting 
of consolidated current assets including undrawn borrowing capacity to 
consolidated current liabilities, of not less than 1.0 to 1.0 as of the last day
of any fiscal quarter;</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-
indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>a maximum leverage ratio, consisting 
of consolidated Revolving Facility Debt to adjusted consolidated EBITDAX (as 
defined in the Credit Facility), of not greater than 4.0 to 1.0 as of the last 
day of any fiscal quarter;</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-
indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>a minimum interest coverage ratio, 
consisting of EBITDAX to Consolidated Interest Expense (as defined in the Credit
Facility), of not less than 2.0 to 1.0 as of the last day of any fiscal quarter;
and</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-
indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>an asset coverage ratio, consisting 
of PV9% to Total Debt (as defined in the Credit Facility), of not less than 1.25
to 1.0, through 2016 and not less than 1.50 to 1.0 thereafter.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subsequent to 30 June&nbsp;2015 and through the date 
of this report, the Company drew $30.0 million on the Revolving Facility, 
bringing the total outstanding to $60.0 million and an undrawn capacity of $15.0
million.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"

derivative financial instruments resulting in a loss of $5.6 million have been 
recognised in the statement of profit or loss and other comprehensive income 
within loss on derivative financial instruments. The interest rate swap 
derivative financial instruments was settled during the period and $0.1 million 
has been recognised in the statement of profit or loss and other comprehensive 
income within other (expense) / income.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SUNDANCE ENERGY AUSTRALIA LIMITED ACN
112 202 883 AND CONTROLLED ENTITIES</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SELECTED EXPLANATORY NOTES TO THE 
FINANCIAL STATEMENTS</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">For the half-year ended 30 
June&nbsp;2015</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NOTE 10 &#151; FAIR VALUE 
MEASUREMENT</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following table presents financial assets and 
liabilities measured at fair value in the statement of financial position in 
accordance with the fair value hierarchy.&#160; This hierarchy groups financial 
assets and liabilities into three levels based on the significance of inputs 
used in measuring the fair value of the financial assets and liabilities. The 
fair value hierarchy has the following levels:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Level 1:</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160; </font>quoted prices (unadjusted) in active markets for 
identical assets or liabilities;</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-
indent:-.75in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">Level 2:</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160; </font>inputs other than quoted prices included within Level 1 
that are observable for the asset or liability, either directly (i.e. as prices)
or indirectly (i.e. derived from prices); and</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;text-
indent:-.75in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">Level 3:</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160; </font>inputs for the asset or liability that are not based on 
observable market data (unobservable inputs).</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Level within which the financial asset or 
liability is classified is determined based on the lowest level of significant 
input to the fair value measurement.&#160; The financial assets and liabilities 
measured at fair value in the statement of financial position are grouped into 
the fair value hierarchy as follows:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New 
Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Consolidated 30 
June&nbsp;2015</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="96%" style="border-
collapse:collapse;margin-left:.25in;">
<tr>
<td width="38%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:38.96%;">

face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-
weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>    </td>
<td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.58%;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font 
size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;font-

<td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.58%;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"

FINANCIAL STATEMENTS</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">For the half-year ended 30 
June&nbsp;2015</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NOTE 10 &#151; FAIR VALUE MEASUREMENT
(CONT)</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Measurement of Fair 
Value</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">a)&#160; Derivatives</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Derivatives entered into by the Company consisted of 
commodity contracts and interest rate swaps.&#160; The Company utilises present 
value techniques and option-pricing models for valuing its derivatives.&#160; 
Inputs to these valuation techniques include published forward prices, 
volatilities, and credit risk considerations, including the incorporation of 
published interest rates and credit spreads.&#160; All of the significant inputs
are observable, either directly or indirectly; therefore, the Company&#146;s 
derivative instruments are included within the Level 2 fair value 
hierarchy.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">b)&#160; Credit 
Facilities</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">As at 30 June&nbsp;2015, the Company had $30 million 
and $125 million of principal debt outstanding on the Revolving Facilities and 
the Term Loans, respectively. The estimated fair value of the Revolving Facility
approximated its carrying amount due to the floating interest rate paid on such 
debt to be set for a period of three months or less.&#160; The estimated fair 
value of the Term Loans was approximately $185 million, based on indirect, 
observable inputs (Level 2) regarding interest rates available to the Company. 
The fair value of the Term Loans was determined by using a discounted cash flow 
model using a discount rate that reflects the Company&#146;s assumed borrowing 
rate at the end of the reporting period.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">c)&#160; Other Financial 
Instruments</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The carrying amounts of cash, accounts receivable, 
accounts payable and accrued liabilities approximate fair value due to their 
short-term nature.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NOTE 11 - ISSUED 
CAPITAL</font></b></p>

style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Total ordinary shares issued at each year end are 
fully paid.</font></p>

style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

style="font-size:10.0pt;">Ordinary shares participate in dividends and the

hands.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Restricted Share Units</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the six month period ended 30 June&nbsp;2015, 
the shareholders and Board of Directors granted 2,809,479 of short term 
incentive restricted share units and 3,090,226 and 7,082,683 of long term 
incentive restricted share units (RSUs) to our CEO and certain other employees, 
respectively (total of 10,172,909 RSUs).&#160; The STI RSUs and LTI RSUs granted
to certain employees, other than our CEO, were granted, but not issued during 
the period.&#160; All RSU awards were made in accordance with the long term 
equity component of the Company&#146;s incentive compensation plan and include 
1,545,113 and 2,815,681 of total shareholder return (TSR) RSUs issued to our CEO
and certain other employees, respectively (total of 4,360,794).&#160; The 
details of the plan and TSR RSUs are described in more detail in the 
remuneration section of the Directors&#146; Report of the Company&#146;s Annual 
Report for the year ended 31 December&nbsp;2014. Share based payment expense for
RSUs awarded was calculated pursuant to AASB 2: Share Based Payments.&#160; The 
fair values of RSUs were estimated at the date they were approved by the 
shareholders and granted to employees, except for the TSR RSUs, which were 
deemed to be immaterial for the six month period ended 30 June&nbsp;2015.&#160; 
This information is summarised for the Consolidated Group for the six month 
period ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 below:</font></p>

style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subsequent to 30 June&nbsp;2015, the 942,860 of RSUs 
vested as at 30 June&nbsp;2015 were converted to ordinary shares.&#160; As 
discussed above, all of the Company&#146;s outstanding options were converted to
1,275,000 RSUs subsequent to 30 June&nbsp;2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>TSR RSUs 
granted during the six month period ended 30 June&nbsp;2015 were deemed to be 
immaterial and do not have an estimated fair value included in the table.&#160; 
The Company&#146;s valuation of these TSR RSUs granted in 2015 will be finalized
prior to issuance of the Company&#146;s 2015 annual report and the appropriate 
portion of the estimated grant date fair value will be recognized as share-based
compensation included in general and administrative expense in the 
Company&#146;s statement of profit or loss and other comprehensive income.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Upon vesting, and after a certain administrative 
period, the RSUs are converted to unrestricted ordinary shares.&#160; As the 
daily closing price of the Company&#146;s shares approximate its estimated fair 
value at that time, the Company used the grant date closing price to estimate 
the fair value of the RSUs.</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SUNDANCE ENERGY AUSTRALIA LIMITED ACN
112 202 883 AND CONTROLLED ENTITIES</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SELECTED EXPLANATORY NOTES TO THE 
FINANCIAL STATEMENTS</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">For the half-year ended 30 
June&nbsp;2015</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NOTE 13 &#151; OPERATING 
SEGMENTS</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s strategic focus is the exploration,
development and production of large, repeatable onshore resource plays in North 
America, which is the Company&#146;s only major line of business and only major 
geographic area of operations. All of the basins and/or formations in which the 
Company operates have common operational characteristics, challenges and 
economic characteristics.&#160; As such, Management has determined, based upon 
the reports reviewed by the Chief Operating Decision Maker (&#147;CODM&#148;) 
and used to make strategic decisions, that the Company has one reportable 
segment being oil and natural gas exploration and production in North 
America.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s CODM is its chief executive officer
(CEO). The CEO reviews internal management reports on a monthly basis that are 
consistent with the information provided in the statement of profit or loss and 
other comprehensive income, statement of financial position and statement of 
cash flows.&#160; As a result, no reconciliation is required, because the 
information as presented is used by the CEO to make strategic 
decisions.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NOTE 14 &#151; CONTINGENT ASSETS AND 
LIABILITIES</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At</font> the date of signing this report, 
the Group is not aware of any significant contingent assets or liabilities that 
should be recognised or disclosed in accordance with AASB 137 &#151; 
<i>Provisions, Contingent Liabilities and Contingent Assets /</i> IFRS 37 - 
Provisions, Contingent Liabilities and Contingent Assets.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NOTE 15 &#151; EVENTS AFTER THE 
REPORTING PERIOD</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Prior to 30 June&nbsp;2015, the Company entered into a
Share and Asset Sale Agreement (&#147;SSA&#148;) for the acquisition of New 
Standard Energy Ltd&#146;s (NSE) U.S (Eagle Ford assets) and Cooper Basin assets
(PEL570).&#160; Upon execution of the SSA, the Company paid approximately 
A$243,000 to NSE for 122 million shares of Elixir Petroleum (ASX: EXR).&#160; 
This investment is included in other current assets in the Company&#146;s 
statement of financial position as at 30 June&nbsp;2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company completed the transaction in 
August&nbsp;2015.&#160; The Eagle Ford assets acquired include approximately 
5,500 net acres in Atascosa County, 7 gross producing wells with approximately 
175 net Boe/d of current production and two wells that have been drilled but not
yet completed.&#160; The Cooper Basin asset acquired is a 17.5% working interest
in the PEL570 concession.&#160; Consideration for the acquisition included $15.0
million to repay NSE&#146;s note with Credit Suisse, the issuance of 6 million 
new fully paid ordinary Company shares and the assumption of net working capital
deficit of approximately $0.9 million.&#160; Included in working capital 
acquired was the fair value of commodity derivative contracts covering 23,000 
barrels of oil at an average floor price of $78 per barrel.&#160; Upon payoff of
the note, Credit Suisse assigned its 2.5% overriding royalty on the Eagle Ford 
assets to the Company.&#160; Approximately 1.5 million of the 6 million Company 
shares will be held in escrow until resolution of due diligence.&#160; The 
Company expects to sell the Cooper Basin asset acquired and 25% of the Eagle 
Ford assets acquired within twelve months of closing.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The initial accounting for the business combination 
was incomplete at the time these financial statements were authorised for 
issue.&#160; Therefore, the fair value of the consideration transferred, assets 
acquired and liabilities assumed in the transaction have not been 
disclosed.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">In August&nbsp;2015, the Company received notice from 
the buyer of its non-operated Phoenix properties sold in December&nbsp;2013 that
they intend to file a lawsuit against the Company.&#160; The claim of $0.9 
million relates to costs not included by the buyer on the final post-closing 
settlement, for which it seeks reimbursement from the Company.&#160; The Company
does not believe the case has merit and, should the lawsuit be filed, intends to
vigorously defend itself.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-
align:center;">18<a name="PB_18_091400_7091"></a></p>

align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"
style="font-size:10.0pt;">To the members of Sundance Energy Australia 
Limited</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Report on the Half-Year Financial 
Report</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">We have reviewed the accompanying half-year financial 
report of Sundance Energy Australia Limited, which comprises the consolidated 
statement of financial position as at 30 June&nbsp;2015, the consolidated income
statement, consolidated statement of comprehensive income, consolidated 
statement of changes in equity and consolidated statement of cash flows for the 
half-year ended on that date, notes comprising a summary of significant 
accounting policies and other explanatory information, and the directors&#146; 
declaration of the consolidated entity comprising the company and the entities 
it controlled at the half-year end or from time to time during the half-
year.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Directors&#146; responsibility for the half-year 
financial report</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">The directors of the company are responsible for the 
preparation of the half-year financial report that gives a true and fair view in
accordance with Australian Accounting Standards and the <i>Corporations Act 
</i>2001 and for such internal controls that the directors determine are 
necessary to enable the preparation of the half year financial report that is 
free from material misstatement, whether due to fraud or error.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Auditor&#146;s responsibility</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our responsibility is to express a conclusion on the 
half-year financial report based on our review. We conducted our review in 
accordance with Auditing Standard on Review Engagements ASRE 2410 <i>Review of a
Financial Report Performed by the Independent Auditor of the Entity</i>, in 
order to state whether, on the basis of the procedures described, we have become
aware of any matter that makes us believe that the financial report is not in 
accordance with the <i>Corporations Act 2001</i> including: giving a true and 
fair view of the consolidated entity&#146;s financial position as at 30 
June&nbsp;2015 and its performance for the half-year ended on that date; and 
complying with Accounting Standard AASB 134 <i>Interim Financial Reporting</i> 
and the <i>Corporations Regulations 2001</i>.&#160; As the auditor of Sundance 
Energy Australia Limited and the entities it controlled during the half-year, 
ASRE 2410 requires that we comply with the ethical requirements relevant to the 
audit of the annual financial report.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">A review of a half-year financial report consists of 
making enquiries, primarily of persons responsible for financial and accounting 
matters, and applying analytical and other review procedures. A review is 
substantially less in scope than an audit conducted in accordance with 
Australian Auditing Standards and consequently does not enable us to obtain 
assurance that we would become aware of all significant matters that might be
identified in an audit. Accordingly, we do not express an audit 
opinion.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Independence</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">In conducting our review, we have complied with the 
independence requirements of the <i>Corporations Act 2001</i>. We have given to 
the directors of the company a written Auditor&#146;s Independence Declaration, 
a copy of which is included in the Directors&#146; Report.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

align:center;">20<a name="PB_20_091609_4141"></a></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Conclusion</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Based on our review, which is not an audit, we have 
not become aware of any matter that makes us believe that the half-year 
financial report of Sundance Energy Australia Limited is not in accordance with 
the <i>Corporations Act 2001</i>, including:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 21.3pt;text-indent:-21.3pt;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">a) giving a true and fair view 
of the consolidated entity&#146;s financial position as at 30 June&nbsp;2015 and
of its performance for the half-year ended on that date; and</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 21.3pt;text-indent:-21.3pt;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">b) complying with Accounting 
Standard AASB 134 <i>Interim Financial Reporting</i> and the <i>Corporations 
Regulations 2001</i>.</font></p>
